  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_658a8717-73a4-4b3a-8932-afb2d1ee3cf6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

              <span id="reviewTextContainer656768034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8088870050736741450"><u> Things I’ve learnt from new-adult Bad Boys (BB)</u><br/><br/>1. A BB never wears underwear under sexy jeans.<br/><br/>2. Only medium to zero confidence can attract a BB.<br/><br/>3. If you are a virgin, or almost, your chances to catch the eye of a BB, triple.<br/><br/>4. After some ruff patches, the BB is no longer a BB, but a SLP (sweet little poodle).<br/><br/>5. You will definitely hit it off with the best friend, who is a BB too, but will also become a SLP, probably in the next book. <br/><br/>6. The BB's bitchy-(but-sexier-than-you)-ex-girlfriend will</span>
  <span id="freeText8088870050736741450" style="display:none"><u> Things I’ve learnt from new-adult Bad Boys (BB)</u><br /><br />1. A BB never wears underwear under sexy jeans.<br /><br />2. Only medium to zero confidence can attract a BB.<br /><br />3. If you are a virgin, or almost, your chances to catch the eye of a BB, triple.<br /><br />4. After some ruff patches, the BB is no longer a BB, but a SLP (sweet little poodle).<br /><br />5. You will definitely hit it off with the best friend, who is a BB too, but will also become a SLP, probably in the next book. <br /><br />6. The BB's bitchy-(but-sexier-than-you)-ex-girlfriend will definitely give you trouble.<br /><br />7. If he is a musician, the BB will write you a song. If he is not, he will find some other way to very publicly announce his affection.<br /><br />8. The BB will definitely mess up. But... just this one time. Afterwards he will definitely beg. <br /><br />9. Casual relationships are not the BB’s style. Only marriage can suffice.<br /><br />10. He will under no circumstances let you wear this little cute black dress. He will demand something from your grandma’s closet or more preferably, the BB will BUY you something in the lines of maternity clothes. <br /><br />11. The BB has to punch every male that breaths in your direction.<br /><br /> <i>And more importantly.. he is not really a BB.. he just didn’t find the right girl..till now, of course..</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8088870050736741450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_667339753" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/667339753" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/667339753?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667339753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18178650140755356889"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429137i/859351._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429137i/859352._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>
      <strong>"So congratulations. You're married to a rock star."</strong>
    </b>
  </em>
</blockquote><br/><b>I'd been wishing for a new rock star book and this one hit the spot and rocked my world!! </b><br/><br/><strong><i>Lick</i> is an addictive blend of heart-warming passion and light-hearted fun. It's a story you can lose yourself in. The perfect rock star romance! 5 stars!</strong><br/><br/>This book had one of the all-time best beginnings ever. I challenge anyone to try and stop reading after the first page!<br/><br/>Evelyn wakes up one morning with a killer hangover and painfu</span>
  <span id="freeText18178650140755356889" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429137i/859351._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429137i/859352._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <em>
    <b>
      <strong>"So congratulations. You're married to a rock star."</strong>
    </b>
  </em>
</blockquote><br><b>I'd been wishing for a new rock star book and this one hit the spot and rocked my world!! </b><br><br><strong><i>Lick</i> is an addictive blend of heart-warming passion and light-hearted fun. It's a story you can lose yourself in. The perfect rock star romance! 5 stars!</strong><br><br>This book had one of the all-time best beginnings ever. I challenge anyone to try and stop reading after the first page!<br><br>Evelyn wakes up one morning with a killer hangover and painfully fuzzy memories, in bed with a gorgeous, heavily inked man she doesn't remember with his name tattooed on her body and a giant sparkling diamond on her finger. Needless to say, this happened in Vegas ;)<br><br>From the very beginning, my heart was already breaking a little for this guy though because he clearly remembered what had happened despite her mindblank.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <em>"Let me get this straight, you don't remember anything?"</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"No," I said, swallowing hard. "What did we do last night?"</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"We got fucking married." he growled.</em>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>After getting over the shock she's faced with the question... to divorce or not to divorce??<br><br>Plan A involved just trying to put everything behind her but she got about as far as the plane before she was hounded by hordes of paparazzi. Turns out that her mystery husband was not only in a band but in a world-famous-fall-on-your-knees-and-worship-them kind of band and by this point literally <em>everyone</em> on the planet (except her still) knew a version of what happened that night.<br><br>So Plan B came into effect and off she headed back to his place to try and settle things that way...<br><blockquote>
  <em>Me: Private jet was amazing. Though his fans are crazy…</em>
  <br>
  <em>Lauren: Whatever happens, do not break up the band!!!</em>
  <br>
  <em>Me: Got it.</em>
  <br>
  <em>Lauren: But break his heart. He wrote San Pedro after what's-her-face cheated on him. That album was BRILLIANT!</em>
  <br>
  <em>Me: Promise to leave him a broken quivering mess.</em>
  <br>
  <em>Lauren: That's the spirit.</em>
  <br>
  <em>Me: xx.</em>
</blockquote><br>But she'd stepped into a crazy rock star world. No one was pleased at her new role in it, she just wanted out, and she couldn't read David but he sure as hell just seemed plain unhappy. But I loved that Ev took it all in stride. Sure, it was overwhelming at times but she was such a strong character and didn't let anything bring her down.<br><br>There was, however, something undeniable between them. A spark... something 'more'. So they took the weekend to give them a second chance to explore that feeling between them that just felt so 'right'.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"I… actually, I'd like to be alone for a minute."</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>He made a growly noise and suddenly his arms wrapped around me, pulling me in against him. He caught me off guard and I stumbled, my nose bumping into his chest. It hurt. Bur he smelled good. Clean, male, and good. Familiar. Some part of me remembered being this close to him and it was comforting. Something in my mind said 'safe'. But I couldn't remember how or why.</em>
</blockquote><br>I totally fell for David. Everything about him just made my heart melt. He was just so sweet and tender. Definite swoon material but at the same time, my heart broke for him...<br><blockquote>
  <strong>
    <em>"It's not fair that I remember and you don't, Evelyn."</em>
  </strong>
</blockquote><br>Ev was a refreshingly down-to-earth, non-ditzy, understanding heroine. I honestly did not feel frustrated with her even once. I respected her decisions and loved the way she handled everything.<br><br>The writing was so real! This author had a way of describing things that put you 'right there' in the moment seeing everything play out in front of your eyes. It was witty, smooth flowing with just the right touch of snark to keep me smiling throughout.<br><br>Ok - now here's what really and truly made this book GOLD to me. The characters were just so <em>functional</em><em>!! </em>Never once did I want to throttle anyone or throw the book at the wall.  Now, don't get me wrong, there was heart-break, the characters messed up and it was certainly not all sunshine and rainbows but the way they reacted to everything was believable and never over-the-top.<br><br>I also loved that the drama in this one was very personal. Yes, he was a world-famous rockstar but the issues here were all very relationship focused and 'internal' having to do with "them", not with paparazzi or his fame or anything.<br><br>I was totally connected to the characters every step of the way. I was happy when they were happy and my heart broke along side theirs.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"Love isn't always smooth or straightforward. It can be messy and painful," he said. "Doesn't mean it still isn't the most incredible thing that can ever happen to you."</em>
</blockquote><br>I loved that they talked through their issues. I loved that there was no instant forgiveness and yet at the same time nothing was dragged out. It felt very balanced to me. Their healing after the heart-break was very believably paced and so by the end, I really felt that their happy ending had a foundation.<br><blockquote>
  <em>"His hands cupped my face, holding me to him. The kiss was so sweet and perfect. It was a promise, one that wouldn't be broken this time. We'd both learned from our mistakes and we'd keep learning all our lives."</em>
</blockquote><br>This is a book about taking chances and following your heart and dreams. It was a feel-good rock star romance with just the right amount of everything you could possibly want in one.<br><br><b> Seriously guys, this book has no game-playing, no stupidity, no unnecessary drama, believable issues, and understandable reactions. It has very "real" characters who make mistakes and yet try to fix them. It was a great blend of warm fuzzies, hotness and heart ache with a wonderfully happy ending that took it's time and made me 'believe'. Bottom line... I loved it!!<br><br>Highly recommended! </b><br><br>PS - this is the first book in a series but it reads as a standalone. No cliffhanger. Each book will be about a different couple and I can't wait for the next in the series!<br><br>Casting (see above and below):<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429137i/859353._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="18178650140755356889" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/672769415" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/672769415?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2020-audio">2020-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672769415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7548111298841148910"><b>4.5 Lickable Stars!!! </b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/30d285bf-e9c0-416b-93d1-9601e90cdd6b_zps020e7a2a.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861629.jpg' alt=' photo 30d285bf-e9c0-416b-93d1-9601e90cdd6b_zps020e7a2a.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was such a fun and sweet book! A really enjoyable read! <br/><br/>Going out for her 21st birthday, Evelyn wants to get a little wild, have a little fun. So she goes to Vegas with her best friend. The last thing she remembers is taking shots after midnight... the next morning she wakes up with a ring on her finger and a tattoo on her ass. And she can't remember a damn thing.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f5430136-1a83-4ff4-ba03-4e90439dd82d_zps46a0cf13.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861630.jpg' alt=' photo f5430136-1a83-4ff4-ba03-4e90439dd82d_zps46a0cf13.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>All I know is if I woke up married to this guy with a 5 carat rock on my finger, I would be asking </span>
  <span id="freeText7548111298841148910" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Lickable Stars!!! </b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/30d285bf-e9c0-416b-93d1-9601e90cdd6b_zps020e7a2a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861629.jpg" alt=" photo 30d285bf-e9c0-416b-93d1-9601e90cdd6b_zps020e7a2a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was such a fun and sweet book! A really enjoyable read! <br><br>Going out for her 21st birthday, Evelyn wants to get a little wild, have a little fun. So she goes to Vegas with her best friend. The last thing she remembers is taking shots after midnight... the next morning she wakes up with a ring on her finger and a tattoo on her ass. And she can't remember a damn thing.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/f5430136-1a83-4ff4-ba03-4e90439dd82d_zps46a0cf13.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861630.jpg" alt=" photo f5430136-1a83-4ff4-ba03-4e90439dd82d_zps46a0cf13.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All I know is if I woke up married to this guy with a 5 carat rock on my finger, I would be asking NO QUESTIONS at all ;)<br><br>David remembers everything, yet Evelyn can’t remember a thing... It hurts him.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘David, you’re hedging. Come on. It’s not fair that you remember and I don’t.’<br><br>‘No, it’s not fair that I remember and you don’t, Evelyn.’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Evelyn has her life mapped out. Getting married to a rockstar she just met on her 21st birthday is not part of that plan. David isn’t happy that Evelyn doesn’t remember anything. He married her for a reason, he fell for her right away, and now he doesn’t know what to do about it. It’s a pretty messed up situation. Once the media catches wind of this its even more crazy. Ev and David go away for a bit to get away from the crowds and decide what to do. To divorce or not to divorce... that is the question. <br><br>While at David’s home away, the couple starts to get to know one another. Evelyn realizes that she really likes David. She may even be falling for him. She is afraid to tell him her feelings. David still feels hurt and betrayed that Evelyn remembers nothing of their night together. One thing is pretty obvious... they both want each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d536e2f0-c05a-4914-85e7-5426e1eae9c1_zps87537938.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861631.jpg" alt=" photo d536e2f0-c05a-4914-85e7-5426e1eae9c1_zps87537938.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>David + Evelyn = super hot chemistry! They decide to make a go of their relationship. <br><i>
  <blockquote>damn the consequences, you know you can probably fly. If you can’t, imagine the thrill of the fall.</blockquote>
</i><br>Once they go back to LA, everything changes. There are a lot of issues, miscommunications etc. Things get screwed up. It’s a little heart breaking. David and Ev spend some time apart, but David realizes...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/41980faf-e816-4966-8140-a98801ba835c_zps8857c012.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429913i/861632.jpg" alt=" photo 41980faf-e816-4966-8140-a98801ba835c_zps8857c012.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why don’t you go back to LA?”<br> “My wife lives in Portland.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Was this the biggest mistake of their lives, or are these two truly meant to be???<br><b>
  <blockquote>‘It’s you and me against the world.’</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I LOVE ROCKSTAR BOOKS! David Ferris was pretty amazing. This was so entertaining, I couldn’t put it down. David wasn’t perfect, he made some mistakes, but neither was Ev. They were, however, better together than apart. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘I married you, Evelyn, because you made sense to me. We make sense. We’re a whole lot better together than apart. You notice that?’<br><br>‘Yeah, I really did.’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Evelyn had her annoying moments, but overall I really liked her. Lick was told from her pov. She was a genuine person, down to earth, real, and pretty hilarious at times. David was just too damn lickable. Hot. Sweet. Swoony. Sexy. Loved him! Their relationship was unconventional, far from perfect, but it worked for them. I loved the two of them together. Sometimes, opposites really do attract. David needs someone to keep him grounded, and Evelyn needs someone to get her to break out of her comfort zone, following her plan isn’t the most important thing in life. <br><br>I’m so glad this is a series... I am very excited to read a Mal book! Fun, sweet, hilarious, sexy, feel-good read! Just a touch of drama and angst, but not overkill. A wonderful rockstar book that will keep a smile on your face!</span>

          </span>

But….just roll with it and think…hey ANYTHING IS POSSIBLE IN FICTION…right!!!!...you begin to enjoy turning the pages, meeting some interesting and quirky characters….Mal (loved this guy) and Jimmy (David’s OOC (out of control) brother….both band members and their stories should be quite fun and interesting (hey, they are going to get their own book, right????). <br><br>The dialogue was a bit “out there” but after a while, I got into it and just went with the flow!!!!<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427663i/855023.jpg" alt=" photo images8_zps19505c30.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>Oh man….so many times I thought of that title…you know the one…..LICK!!!! <div id="review_661859667" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/661859667" />
    <a title="La-Lionne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne"><img alt="La-Lionne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458815714p2/11644154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/661859667?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="La-Lionne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="La-Lionne" href="/user/show/11644154-la-lionne">La-Lionne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=reviews-say-yay-i-say-nay">reviews-say-yay-i-say-nay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=skipped-a-lot">skipped-a-lot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=i-could-have-written-this-book">i-could-have-written-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=dumb-heroine">dumb-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=bad-boy-ish">bad-boy-ish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer661859667" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13581896629174506896">I'm not sure what to say about this book. I didn't hate it, but didn't love it either. Since there were more things that I disliked than I liked, two stars is more than fair.<br/><br/>-WARNING SPOILERS-<br/><br/>The story had a solid beginning. After I read the first chapter I was very exited. I was sure it will be at least a 4 star read. <br/>Ev wakes up one morning, in a hotel room in Vegas, with the biggest hangover of her life, a wedding ring on her finger and a tattoo with a name "David" on her ass, with no memory </span>
  <span id="freeText13581896629174506896" style="display:none">I'm not sure what to say about this book. I didn't hate it, but didn't love it either. Since there were more things that I disliked than I liked, two stars is more than fair.<br /><br />-WARNING SPOILERS-<br /><br />The story had a solid beginning. After I read the first chapter I was very exited. I was sure it will be at least a 4 star read. <br />Ev wakes up one morning, in a hotel room in Vegas, with the biggest hangover of her life, a wedding ring on her finger and a tattoo with a name "David" on her ass, with no memory of how all of those things happened. Uh-oh :-).<br />She came to Las Vegas with her friend to let loose and have fun and took things a little too far. <br />The guy next to her in bed is gorgeous, shoulder-long dark hair, well build, tattoos all over, just how I like 'em :-). The problem is she doesn't know who he is or how he got there. <br />David is being nice and attentive, while she is freaking out, understandably. They exchange few awkward sentences, she throws up on him a time or two before running out to catch a plane home. <br />When she get's to Portland she gets a shock of her life when paparazzies attack her at the airport asking all kinds of weird questions.<br />Here I thought "Let the good times roll" :-D. I knew they would end up together eventually, I just thought that I will have a blast reading about them going at each other, hating each other, fighting, while discovering things that they liked about one another and falling in love.. It was nothing of sort.<br /><br />The more I read the more it seemed that the Ev in the first chapter and Ev in the rest of the book were two completely different characters. The first one sounded fun and adventurous, the Ev in the rest of the book was wishy washy, whining drama queen. <br />For me things went south after she went to his place to sign the divorce papers. I thought it was annoying when she started to call him her husband. I understand that technically he was her husband, but the way she kept saying it made it sound like she owned him, like they've been married for years or something. <br />I didn't like that they patched things up so soon. The words "true love" were used 3 days into their marriage :-S. Seriously??? <br /><br />To my disappointment, the high point of the story was when Ev walked in on David being kissed by Amanda. It was no-brainer, she walked in on something that wasn't what it looked like, but author made this huge drama out of it and dragged it on and on through the rest of the story. I'm so sick of this type of drama, it has been done a million times over, come up with something more creative. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>Ev:</u>
</b><br />She is a weird one. I'm going to echo what my RB Alex said, she is geeky, and not in a sexy way. I also thought that her wording was very strange. <br /><b>
  <blockquote>"His gaze lingered on my breasts until finally he dipped his head, taking one into his mouth."</blockquote>
</b> Sh!t! The whole thing??? Either her breasts are very small or he has a huge mouth :-S.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Without fuss he dealt with the condom."</blockquote>
</b> I've never heard anyone making a fuss about disposing a condom. Ev made it sound like there was something to make fuss about, but David, being a gentleman that he is, never did. Was there something that author left unsaid? Did condom exploded? What happened? I want to know!<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"I really didn't need him catching me sniffing at his crotch, no matter how poetic my thoughts. That would be embarrassment on a scale I'd prefer not to experience."</blockquote>
</b><br />First of all, I think there is a word missing there. Alex? Second, Ev, you make it sound like sniffing guys crotches is unheard of. I do it all the time :-D :-D :-D.<br />But seriously, why would you want to sniff his crotch? That's the question of the day. Were there bees buzzing around it and you thought it might smell like honey?<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"He didn't have much of a belly button. It was basically a small indent followed by a fine trail of dark hair leaning down across his flat stomach directly to <i>it</i>. And <i>it</i> was hard, thick, and long.<br /><i>It</i> being his penis, of course."</blockquote>
</b> Of course! Phew, thank god it was his penis. For a second there I thought that scary ass raccoon will pop out from under the covers :-D. <br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Face to face with my girly bits."</blockquote>
</b> Freaky stuff. Her girly bits have a face :-S. I think I saw a scary movie once, where girls vagina had teeth. The face thing sounds almost as scary :-S.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"People in love were sickening. It was a proven medical fact."</blockquote>
</b> Who proved it ? I wanna a name!<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"I tucked my hair behind my ears because my ponytail had started falling apart again. Perfect metaphor for my life."</blockquote>
</b> I don't know about it being a perfect metaphor, but it will do if you can't come up with a better one.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"He tramped up the stairs behind me, not really bothering to look around."</blockquote>
</b><br />First of all, why would he be looking around? It's not like you lived in a cave. And second, how would you know he never looked around, he was walking behind you?<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Does your heart understands you're finished with her? I guess I mean your head, don't I?"</blockquote>
</b> Beats the hell outta me. Who the hell knows what you mean anymore. I should have stop trying to understand a long time ago :-S.<br /><br />There were couple wtf moments. The biggest one was when she almost had a stroke when she saw David's erection twitch. Funniest thing ever :-D. I would recommend to read this book for that scene alone.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"His c@ck twitched and I jerked back, startled."</blockquote>
</b> Scary stuff. I think I would have passed out if I was in her situation, she handled it like a champ. And here I thought raccoon jumping out would have been scary :-D. <br /><br />There were a lot of unnecessary adverbs like "obviously" and "clearly". <br /><br />I'm all for authors getting creative, coming up with new and original phrases, but this one took it a little too far. Which left me confused more often than not. Even kindle dictionary didn't know the meaning of some of them. I was googling the hell out of some of them.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"I felt curiously naked with him now," ?<br />"Curiosity got the better of me, or maybe it already had." ?<br />"My spine snapped to attention."? <br />"It made me small and shut me down inside."?<br />"as per my usual modus operandi"</blockquote>
</b> I'm not sure what that means, but it sounds very cool :-D.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Face screwed up in confusion"</blockquote>
</b> Sounds very cartoonish. <br />For a girl that couldn't come up with a better word for David's penis than "it" you, Ev, used a lot of big words. "Minuscule", "omnipotent" and "discombobulated". Now that's funny :-D.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>David:</u>
</b><br />He is not your typical rock star. He doesn't have a single bad-boy bone in his body. His personality is too mellow and too vanilla for a persona like him. I liked him at first, but soon he jumped on the same train with Ev, heading for town Weird-Phrases-Big-Words-and-Things-That-Make-Little-To-No-Sence.<br /><br />My problems with him tarted when Ev walked in on him and Amanda, and when he stood there speechless, mouth ajar. Then he started shouting for her to leave. Spanish telenovela much?<br />It took him 28 days to come to her. So much for true love :-).<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"I care about your periods, Ev. Honestly to f@ck I do."</blockquote>
</b> That's good to know, David, not a lot of guys do :-D.<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"David: She surprised me when she kissed me. That's why I didn't stop her right away."</blockquote>
</b> If someone would have been trying to suck my face off, my surprised reaction would have been hulk-punch him in the face and ask questions later. That's a slowest surprised reaction ever. It reminded me a little of Ev's none-kick in the balls :-).<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"I didn't kiss you at the studio today because it felt like there was still too much up in the air between us. It didn't feel right."</blockquote>
</b> Oh no? But f@cking her in the alley against the wall wasn't too much too soon? What's the deal with no kissing, people? You sound like a hooker, David :-).<br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Your parents looked about ready to have kittens."</blockquote>
</b> I guess he meant they were angry. I've seen a cat giving birth couple of times and it's not dramatic at all :-). Badass analogy for a badass rock star :-D. Weirdest analogy ever.<br /><br />There was a character that I liked, Mal. He was very cool and funny. I hope he will get his own book. I'll defiantly read it. <br /><br />All and all, it's a two "meh" stars from me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13581896629174506896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16556746484964252755"><b>4 to 4 1/2–I'm glad I gave this book a second chance–Stars<br/><br/>After my first failed attempt to read this book–explained in my original review below–I knew it would be a good idea to put it aside for awhile before giving it another try. Boy, am I glad I decided to give it another go. I loved this book! I loved the characters, the plot, and the love story. I ended this book with a huge smile on my face. </b><br/><br/><u>7/8/13 Revised Review</u><br/><br/>GOODNESS GRACIOUS! Did I ever put my foot in my mouth with my original review </span>
  <span id="freeText16556746484964252755" style="display:none"><b>4 to 4 1/2–I'm glad I gave this book a second chance–Stars<br /><br />After my first failed attempt to read this book–explained in my original review below–I knew it would be a good idea to put it aside for awhile before giving it another try. Boy, am I glad I decided to give it another go. I loved this book! I loved the characters, the plot, and the love story. I ended this book with a huge smile on my face. </b><br /><br /><u>7/8/13 Revised Review</u><br /><br />GOODNESS GRACIOUS! Did I ever put my foot in my mouth with my original review of <i>Lick</i>. Word to the wise, if you know you're an emotional mess from the previous book you've just read, have been up half the night reading your next book and are bone tired, and you're having a difficult time following the plot, maybe it's a good idea to put the book down for the night. Unfortunately, I didn't heed this advice and misconstrued what the author had written. <b>As I read it again with fresh eyes, what I thought was cheating most definitely WAS NOT!!! And I can not stress that enough.</b><br /><br />This book deserves a fair review, as I really enjoyed it up until I created a different sub-plot. That said, I need some time before immersing myself in it again, as, frankly, I tainted it for myself. <br /><br />My apologies to the author, to potential readers, and to those who follow my reviews. <br /><br /><i>A special thanks to Natasha and Jenny for taking the time to help me understand the mistake I made. Both of you are FIRST CLASS!!</i></span>

<div id="review_1753156784" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1753156784" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1753156784?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854208" href="/book/show/18779133-lick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=jealous-sweet-guys">jealous-sweet-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=rock-stars">rock-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1753156784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10105737570090877830"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You made sense to me. We make sense. We're a whole lot better together than apart."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>4 Rock Stars!</b><br/><br/>This book was all I've ever needed in a rock star romance story. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lick</a> was a sweet, fast moving, and guilty-pleasure book that was a pure joy to read.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474109512ra/20554941.gif' width='400' height='190' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story began when <b>Evelyn "Ev" Thomas</b> woke up with a realization that she's married to the famous lead guitarist of <i>Stage Dive</i> band, <b>David Ferris</b>. She happened to forget the details on how she got married to him though, because apparently i</span>
  <span id="freeText10105737570090877830" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You made sense to me. We make sense. We're a whole lot better together than apart."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>4 Rock Stars!</b><br><br>This book was all I've ever needed in a rock star romance story. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17983690.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_" title="Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott" rel="nofollow noopener">Lick</a> was a sweet, fast moving, and guilty-pleasure book that was a pure joy to read.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474109512ra/20554941.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story began when <b>Evelyn "Ev" Thomas</b> woke up with a realization that she's married to the famous lead guitarist of <i>Stage Dive</i> band, <b>David Ferris</b>. She happened to forget the details on how she got married to him though, because apparently it was a drunken marriage that happened in Vegas. Now she is in for a crazy and unexpected ride of her life-- being a Mrs. David Ferris wherein she has to deal with paparazzi stuffs and obsessed fans. And being someone who's confused whether she wants the marriage to continue or not-- given the fact that it was an insta-marriage kind and that David is still a stranger, after all.<br><br>First of all, I loved David. I've read a few rock star stories with equally hot rock star leads but David is quite different. Apart from being a man-candy who has an intoxicating charm all over his body, this guy knows exactly how to care for his woman. I loved the way he extended his sweetness for Ev and the way he chased after her when things got bad. <br><br>Our heroine Ev is also likeable, although I wish to see more depth in her character. Despite the absence of that factor though, I found her feelings for David genuine. She didn't care about how rich and famous David is but instead she treated him like an ordinary guy. As for the side characters, I found them really adorable and interesting-- especially Mal and Jimmy. I can't wait to read their stories in the next books of this series!<br><br>Overall, this book met my expectations. It didn't fail to surprise me and make me smile the whole time I was reading it. I loved that it was just light and easy read, without unnecessary dramas. I also loved how it was written in an enticing and delicious way. It's my first time to read Kylie Scott's work and she sure made me fall in love with her writing style. <br><br><i>(I've read this book for the <b>#NALitLoversPH #NewAdultAndBeyondPH</b> readalong)</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10105737570090877830" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText1778616838928873877" style="display:none"><b>5 Rock Gods, FanGirls &amp; Messy, Sexy Love Stars<br><br><i> Love isn’t always smooth or straightforward. It can be messy and painful,” he said. “Doesn’t mean it isn’t still the most incredible thing that can ever happen to you. Doesn’t mean I’m not crazy about you.”</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430866i/864078._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“Play that lick again, Dave.”</b>
</i><br><br><i><b>Lick:</b> In rock music, a lick is "a stock pattern or phrase" consisting of a short series of notes that is used in solos and melodic lines.</i><br><br>Well, personally, I prefer the more literal meaning...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Hold me<br>Kiss me<br>LICK ME!!</b>
</blockquote><br><br><pre>DAVID FERRIS, YOU CAN LICK ME ANYTIME!</pre><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430866i/864079.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What are the last or maybe the BEST words, a girl is expecting to hear, when she wakes up from an night of partying in Las Vegas with no recollection of the last 12 hours, with a hangover from hell and the first thing she sees, is a gorgeous bare-chested male specimen?<br><br><i>
  <b>“So, congratulations. You’re married to a rock star.”</b>
</i><br><br>Well organized and sensible <b>Evelyn Thomas'</b> life is turned upside down, when she wakes up with a humongous diamond ring on her finger, married to famous <i>Stage Dive’s</i> guitarist <b>David Ferris</b>. But she got nothing to worry, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792297i/561910._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WRONG! So, so wrong...<br>She and David, will unexpectedly find what they were looking for in each other’s arms. Passion, love and understanding. The meaning of their existence and some unexpected truths about themselves.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Damn the consequences, you know you can probably fly. If you can’t, imagine the thrill of the fall.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430866i/864080.png" width="400" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They will come to be each other’s everything and decide to give in to love, until some secrets and rockstar painful truths, will try to pry them apart, breaking their new-found happiness. Will Ev forgive David and give him another chance? Will David fight for her with everything he has and will prove to her that love worths taking a plunge and risk your heart in the process?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430866ra/864081.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My inner fan-girl got loose, had a wild night in Vegas, joined a rock band and fell in love with a ROCKSTAR!!! Sweet Mother of God, WHAT DID I JUST READ???<br>David Ferris and The Stage Dive, made my hormones sing and my very robust reproductive organs, explode. *chuckle*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/612591.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Funny and lighthearted, surprisingly deep and serious at the same time, romantic, heartbreaking and melodic as a rock ballad, this story stole my heart and warmed my soul. Fantastic one-liners, banter and interactions.<br>Highly recommended book; you will obsess, fell in love and despair, as a rock God will try to convince his soul mate, that they belong together. And oh boy, you will pray for him to succeed…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430866i/864082.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_657731497" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/657731497" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/657731497?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer657731497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer322662898348721942"><b>4 DAVID FERRIS STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"so, congratulations. You're married to a rockstar."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427755i/855292._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yes, yes, yes cinderella meets 'what happened in Vegas' meets a rockstar romance all combined to create the best kind of blissful book escape. 'Lick' was full of all kinds of treats, Rock God, famous beyond measure hero sweeps ordinary 21 year old off her feet in a whirl wind romance destined to be forever, did I love this book? You don't even need to ask, it had everything I loved tied up in a rock star package and as f</span>
  <span id="freeText322662898348721942" style="display:none"><b>4 DAVID FERRIS STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"so, congratulations. You're married to a rockstar."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427755i/855292._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, yes, yes cinderella meets 'what happened in Vegas' meets a rockstar romance all combined to create the best kind of blissful book escape. 'Lick' was full of all kinds of treats, Rock God, famous beyond measure hero sweeps ordinary 21 year old off her feet in a whirl wind romance destined to be forever, did I love this book? You don't even need to ask, it had everything I loved tied up in a rock star package and as far as books in this genre go, this came out with a humongous thumbs up from me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427755i/855293._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Whats it all about? (if you haven't already guessed)</b><br>Evelyn 'Ev' Thomas is an ordinary 21 year old looking for fun in Vegas for her birthday, a young woman who lives on the boring, safe side of life finds herself thrown into the limelight when her birthday celebrations are taken a step too far with a certain yummy rock God, David Ferris. David is the lead singer of famous band 'stage dive' looking for that something different from his hectic lifestyle, he meets our heroine and falls head over, as in most books of this genre there is more than meets the eye with this gorgeous hero, a character i'm convinced most readers will fall for. 'Lick' is a predictable but entertaining story which captivates a modern but classic take of a cinderella romance. Will these loveable characters find their perfect ending? ...<br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>David Ferris, David Ferris ... Hmmm David Ferris, you got that? Yes Im not in denial about my crush on this fictional character he was a dreamy book companion and filled out my 4 ish plus hours of reading time quite nicely thank you. But on to other matters of the book, this story filled my need for easy reading perfectly. If you roll your eyes or get a little frustrated at predictable story lines or a little over done before plots then this may grate a little but for me it was what I love about a book, no over angst no unnecessary tears, just pure undiluted easy, peasy, lemon, squeezy reading. The writing style flowed at a lovely pace, it was entertaining and well edited and all around a fun, sweet and sexy book. I can't wait for more from the characters, the author added just the right amount from supporting characters to get me interested in future story lines. <br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>For my reading experience it doesn't really register if a story is unbelievable or fairy style fiction that's why I love reading - to escape to read about lives that are far fetched and dreamy and that's what 'Lick' delivered for me. This story is a great all rounder for those that love a Rock star romance with a slice of sweet and sexy served on the side. Go grab it readers ...<br><br>Just a little more of David AKA I HEART Jared Leto ... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380427755i/855294._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="322662898348721942" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Mr Brightside in The Mighty Storm <br/>Or sometimes things happen, emotions are explained and you think of certain songs… <br/><br/>I thought of a lot of songs while reading this… <br/>So If this book was a musical I think it would go something like this… <br/><br/><i>Today, I woke up, thinking about Elvis somewhere in Vegas<br/>I'm not sure how I got here</i></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>

          added it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669222449" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5643478604595021560"><b>DNF at 61 %. No official rating from moi. When I started reading Lick I said I wouldn't rate it IF I wouldn't like it. I keep my word although I must say it was no more than a two-star read. Review posted July 23, 2013</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429408i/860194.png' alt=' photo Bildschirmfoto2013-07-18um194751_zpsf0a2dd66.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>That's exactly what a lot of authors are doing these days and there is no need to beat around the bush. THAT'S. NOT. GOOD. ENOUGH. FOR. ME.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429408i/860195.png' alt=' photo Bildschirmfoto2013-07-18um195036_zps40e7cc8e.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>The beginning was kinda cute, nothing mind-boggling, nothing amazingly good, but still. What I noticed right off the bat was the constant descr</span>
  <span id="freeText5643478604595021560" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 61 %. No official rating from moi. When I started reading Lick I said I wouldn't rate it IF I wouldn't like it. I keep my word although I must say it was no more than a two-star read. Review posted July 23, 2013</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429408i/860194.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-07-18um194751_zpsf0a2dd66.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's exactly what a lot of authors are doing these days and there is no need to beat around the bush. THAT'S. NOT. GOOD. ENOUGH. FOR. ME.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429408i/860195.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-07-18um195036_zps40e7cc8e.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The beginning was kinda cute, nothing mind-boggling, nothing amazingly good, but still. What I noticed right off the bat was the constant description of David's facial expression. Seriously? I really don't get it why an author would keep on writing about the same ole stuff. The eyebrow thingy or the scowling or whatnot. IT WAS TEDIOUS. This being said, it was good enough until they left to go to his house in Monterey aaaaand the whole thing went down the drain once and for all. I didn't get it why Ev was talking about TRUE LOVE two or three days after she WANTED to sign the divorce papers. Now that was a quick change of mind and so not believable. Overall Lick is another so-called rock star story that was simply 'blah'. Add in the fact that I've read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star" title="How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">How to Kill a Rock Star</a> before I gave Lick a shot and a little disaster was bound to occur. <b>These two books are worlds apart.</b> HtKaRS is the best of the best. In all honesty, I hadn't expected to read another book of this epic magnitude but Lick <s>licked</s> lacked big time. I don't mean to go into details now because I don't want to waste my time by listing all my issues. All I will say is:<br><br>This book bored me and the sex was uninspiring. Besides, the characters were too bland and there was nothing badass about David either. The dialogue was weird at times. Ev talking about "it" made me roll my eyes. Call things as they are. Ev, baby, read my lips. C@ck, dick or whatever. It's not an "it." And a twitching c@ck shouldn't startle you either. You touched his c@ck. What did you expect? As long as no one is going to cut the dick off, <i>"it"</i> will move, you know? *facepalm* <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Cute. Are you on the pill?"<br>(…)<br>"I care about your periods, Ev. Honest to fuck I do." He kissed my cheeks, my forehead.<br>"Thanks."<br>"But right now I wanna know how you feel about us going bare?"<br>"You mean more than losing the shirts, I take it?"<br>"I mean f@cking without a condom."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Um…that's the point where I decided that I've had enough of Ev and <b>
  <i>her husband</i>
</b> and abandoned the book.<br><br>Now we're coming to the good part coz I need a goody to give me solace. I'm a fan of Myles Kennedy and Alter Bridge. The man can sing, he plays a mean guitar and he writes great songs. And let's not forget his sexy arms. Yum! What more could a heart desire?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429408ra/860196.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mf75bn20KV1rm70dxo1_500_zpsb4e88135.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429408ra/860197.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mq1ktvxnA61r45vi1o1_400_zps2a5743ff.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429408ra/860198.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mk4kfxvRvi1rsntc8o1_500_zpsc12e42d9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, Myles doesn't make me whole but he sure makes me happy with his music. Seeing Alter Bridge live was one hell of an experience. Good memories...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429408i/860199.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-07-18um193951_zpsd5f68fa9.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S. The cover was definitely better than the story.<br><br>P.P.S. I liked Mal. The guy was pretty fun and cool.<br><br><br>No need to dwell on it. Onwards...<br></span>

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469809265ra/19860656.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Please note said leading male was actually a member of the long hair don’t care club, but long haired Leto just doesn’t do the same thing for me . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469809265ra/19860657.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Because banging Jesus is probably a cardinal sin.<br><br>But I digress. <br><br>So the story here is that Evelyn goes to Vegas with her bestie for her 21st birthday and decides she’s gonna let her freak flag fly with a one-nighter . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469809265ra/19860658.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Things don’t go quite as planned, however, when she wakes up with her head in a toilet and a 5 carat rock on her left hand. Turns out baby married a rock-n-roller but doesn’t remember a diddly dang dong thing about it. <br><br>Then we enter the pretty typical for a romance category and somehow David the Rock God is totally down with the whole death do us part mumbo jumbo and pretty offended that his wife suffers from a severe case of CRS (that’s Can’t.Remember.Shit for all you classy mah fahs). Buuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuuut, also in typical romance fashion there is a delay in the annulment process and the two fall in instalurv within a few days. And then of course . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469809265ra/19860659.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>WHICH I AM GOING TO SPOIL RIGHT HERE BECAUSE IT’S A DEALBREAKER FOR A LOT OF YOU</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She catches him being kissed by his ex, but of course since everyone in these stories is effing brain damaged they don’t talk about it and instead break up only to get back together for the big HEA.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This was another story that ended up just being okay because of the aforementioned dramatic twist. The sex was pretty sexy – except when he wanted her to watch him while he went downtown. I can live without looking at my own lady garden getting tended thank you very little. It was also refreshingly realistic with respect to how a pretty inexperienced partner would handle her first few trips to Pound Town. But the best part of the whole thing? Mal. I already checked out his story from the library and . . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469809623ra/19860724.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>just thinking about it.<br><br><br><b>ORIGINAL "REVIEW":</b><br><br>It's a <b>WOKE UP MARRIED TO A STRANGER</b> storyline!!!!!<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469647919ra/19840810.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ahhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhhh the most tired of all tired tropes. Me likey : )</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12187452853451466807" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_648642114" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648642114" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648642114?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648642114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4167786275133405424"><b>4 1/2 ~ I Married a Rockstar ~ Stars</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426429i/852085._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='320' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i>Lick (Stage Dive 1)</i> was such a refreshingly done rockstar book. I haven’t read anything by this author but will be checking out her books because I really <b>LOVED</b> Kylie Scott’s writing style!<br/><br/>Kylie Scott can write inner dialogue like no one’s business. I laughed and smiled at how completely hilarious and clever she writes her characters, they seemed so real. To say I enjoy this breath of fresh air would be putting mildly!<br/> <br/>This story grabs a reader from the first </span>
  <span id="freeText4167786275133405424" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 ~ I Married a Rockstar ~ Stars</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426429i/852085._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Lick (Stage Dive 1)</i> was such a refreshingly done rockstar book. I haven’t read anything by this author but will be checking out her books because I really <b>LOVED</b> Kylie Scott’s writing style!<br><br>Kylie Scott can write inner dialogue like no one’s business. I laughed and smiled at how completely hilarious and clever she writes her characters, they seemed so real. To say I enjoy this breath of fresh air would be putting mildly!<br> <br>This story grabs a reader from the first paragraph as our main character Evelyn wakes up in Vegas <b>MARRIED</b>. The beginning kind of reminded me of the 2008 movie <i>What Happens in Vegas</i> which I loved. She wakes with a 5 freaking karat diamond ring on her hand and no recollection of the guy in her hotel room or anything that happened the night before when she was out celebrating her 21st birthday.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426429i/852086._SX540_.jpg" width="320" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Evelyn was such a great female character. She wasn’t the perfect slim character but was curvy and she had me smiling and pleasantly surprised by her strength and heart. Evelyn has a life plan which includes following in her daddy’s footsteps as an architect so when she finds herself looking at the hottest piece of ass she has ever seen…she figures it was just one big drunken mistake and this newlywed couple decides to call it quits. <br><br><b>
  <i>"When a girl like me wakes up married to a guy like you, what else can she possibly think? God, David, look at you. You're beautiful, rich, and successful."</i>
</b><br><br>David Ferris is the <b>HOT</b> guitarist/song writer for the rock back Stage Dive. This reader found him drool worthy! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426429i/852087._SX540_.jpg" width="320" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Here’s a tidbit about David Ferris… he wasn’t too drunk and knew exactly what he was doing in Vegas. <br><br>Do you know what that means?<br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s not fair that I remember you and you don’t, Evelyn.” </i>
</b><br><br>To annul or not to annul that is the question!!<br><br>On a hot scale...David and Ev were down right sexy together. <br><br>Although the miscommunication issue wasn’t unique (I HATE when this happens in books) I have to say that the story was a lot of fun both characters displayed growth and they definitely belong together!!<br><br><b>
  <i>“Only this was real, me and him together. Everything else could come and go. I’d found what was worth fighting for.”</i>
</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426429i/852088._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Lick</i> was a very amusing story with terrific characters (loved Mal) and a terrific couple who was not only off the charts in the bedroom but had a connection worth holding onto. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4167786275133405424" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Being the awesome friend she is <s>who contributes to my wallet bleeding</s>, she told me this book could cure my book hangover/slump and oh boy did I devour this one! ♥ It's been far too long since I read a rockstar romance read and jumping back into it, I realised how much I missed the fun sm</span>
  <span id="freeText727562010181302435" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS! ★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420552164ra/13238386.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yet another impulsive read from me when I saw this book with a yummy cover at my bookstore and first thing I did was snapped a photo and messaged my lovely gurl, Rachel to see if she recc'd me this. Being the awesome friend she is <s>who contributes to my wallet bleeding</s>, she told me this book could cure my book hangover/slump and oh boy did I devour this one! ♥ It's been far too long since I read a rockstar romance read and jumping back into it, I realised how much I missed the fun smexy times of dating one of these bad boys.<br><br>It was a really fun read with hilarious banters all around from the band members like Mal &lt;-- oh yes love him! and David was obviously swoon-worthy. The first half there I was a little apprehensive of how one can be so drunk to the extent of almost suffering amnesia of that night's events LOL. And also insta-love which I wished they would have explored more on instead of taking the love expressway. Took some suspension of disbelief from me but it didn't stop me at all from liking this one.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“With great breasts come great responsibility.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420552298ra/13238390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What made it a solid 4-stars read for me is the angst galore towards the second half. I just ate that up when David had so much grovelling to do to get Evelyn back, so that makes me a very happy angst whore :D <br><br>Overall super fun smexy read of the rockstar romance genre and can't wait to read more from this series! Especially can't wait to meet Mal ♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="727562010181302435" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
