<div id="review_647872100" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/647872100" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/647872100?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">anyone up for a mildly sexy read with fears of growing too attached to the characters</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=rockstars">rockstars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority">i-m-gonna-be-in-the-minority</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer647872100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8700298606989045435"><b>
  <i>2 STARS<br/><blockquote>“Rough sex doesn’t fix everything. Sometimes you actually have to talk.”</blockquote></i>
</b><br/>As much as possible, I try to push myself as a reader, to read beyond comfort zones, expand horizons and challenge my imagination. I've yet to scratch the surface of these wonderful worlds, yet to have read and quoted every heart-wrenching dialogue crafted especially to gut me every imaginable way...<br/><br/>But sometimes, I just want to read some smut.<br/><br/>Not the funny, absurd kind with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/624550980' rel='nofollow noopener'>men who cums jarfuls of semen </a>but the s</span>
  <span id="freeText8700298606989045435" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>2 STARS<br><blockquote>“Rough sex doesn’t fix everything. Sometimes you actually have to talk.”</blockquote></i>
</b><br>As much as possible, I try to push myself as a reader, to read beyond comfort zones, expand horizons and challenge my imagination. I've yet to scratch the surface of these wonderful worlds, yet to have read and quoted every heart-wrenching dialogue crafted especially to gut me every imaginable way...<br><br>But sometimes, I just want to read some smut.<br><br>Not the funny, absurd kind with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/624550980" rel="nofollow noopener">men who cums jarfuls of semen </a>but the smut that calls to the romantic in me that answers the call of the hot, tattooed rockstar... Like the Thundercats answering Lion-O.<br><br>Unfortunately, I am not a Thundercat (dammit!) and while the lure of sex, drugs and rock and roll is strong on this one, I could not switch off that part of me that needs to connect with the characters, to make sense of their actions and thoughts that enables me to empathize with their requisite drama and share in their joy as they triumph against all odds.<br><br>I thought the premise of <i>Lick</i> was promising: a girl wakes up in Vegas married to a rockstar without any such recollection on their wedding night. Mixing rock and roll with matrimony always end up with something interesting. John and Yoko, Mick and Bianca, Tommy and Pamela... Need I go on? So the first chapter really hooked me in, because the possibilities of squee and shenanigans was endless as Evelyn, the plain, country music loving heroine, tries to piece together her night of debauchery with a stranger who turns out to be rock icon David Ferris.<br><br>The succeeding chapters called for some meditating with my <b>
  <i>WHAT WOULD BRITNEY DO</i>
</b> bracelet.<br><br>If I found out a total stranger married me while I was drunk, while KNOWING full well I was drunk, I probably would've demand for a divorce then go back home. Which was what Ev did. Yay Ev!<br><br>But probably not get on a private plane to LA immediately after landing from Vegas, back to the stranger I married, in order to escape the paparazzi camped at my house. To sign my divorce papers.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426317i/851756.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From there every scene was solely between David and Evelyn, which was good for the steam factor but not for either characters' personality details. They never spent any time apart longer than a few pages, and when they do, you could smell the contrived plot device to have one of them turn up unannounced two paragraphs in. I was around 50% in when I realized I don't know enough about these people to care about their drama. Who was Evelyn the daughter? The friend? The sister? Who is David beyond his fame and fortune? Where does his principle stand on the lifestyle he's in? What's their stand on same-sex marriage and the genocide in Uganda?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426317ra/851757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Something. Anything for me to latch on to care beyond the sex. Some of these questions did get answered. In the end. At which point I was too exhausted to care and suddenly giving a damn about these people felt moot with only a chapter to go. Sadly, the only character who I felt like I understood was Martha because her actions at least bore some semblance of logic.<br><br>I also felt the story failed to capitalize on two of its strongest plot points: David and Ev's drunk marriage and David and Jimmy's relationship. The former got resolved halfway through the book putting a kibosh on the tension (which is always the best part) and just going all out on the sexeh (which was mediocre at best). I found the David and Jimmy dynamics to be severely lacking, in terms of being band mates and brothers. Who didn't pick a side between Liam and Noel Gallagher? That little nugget of conflict could have powered this book on its own but wasn't exploited much, unfortunately.<br><br>The writing was a bit all over the place. Most of the time it was okay and I didn't get bothered by it, but there were stretches that sounded like Ev needed some Ritalin.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Does your heart understand you’re finished with her? I guess I mean your head, don’t I? The heart’s just another muscle, really. Silly to say it decides anything.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>So many thoughts, so few pages! Furthermore, Ev's inner thoughts have moments that have that brand of strange bordering on funny where I'm not sure if I should laugh or frown.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“He treated me like I was precious. Like I was a china doll. One he could apparently have rough sex with upon occasion.”<br><br>"I needed new panties and a heart transplant."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426317i/851758._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> I feel this would have worked better as a novella, because as a quick and sexy romp this would have totally delivered. I would then just take it for the fun and sexytimes that it did provide and I wouldn't have any material to overanalyze and pick on, no grief to give the cardboard personalities of both leads. But as the plot thickened so did the expectations which, unfortunately this one fell short out of. To modify David's words:<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“With <s>great breasts</s> more pages, come great responsibility.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8700298606989045435" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667511718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13712340883001144316"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859429._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859430._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Eeeeeeee. Love love love it. Soooo perfect. And adorable. And hot. And brilliant.<br/><br/>A fantastic rock star romance. What happens in Vegas, stays in Vegas, right??? Wrong! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859431._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When you accidently get married to one of the biggest rock stars on the planet, the ring, the paparazzi, the legal papers and the hubby himself are all still there, even after you leave Vegas... even if you have absolutely no recollection of the whole thing!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859432._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859433.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Good, respectable, sensible, Portland girl, Evelyn Thomas might have been p</span>
  <span id="freeText13712340883001144316" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859429._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859430._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eeeeeeee. Love love love it. Soooo perfect. And adorable. And hot. And brilliant.<br><br>A fantastic rock star romance. What happens in Vegas, stays in Vegas, right??? Wrong! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859431._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When you accidently get married to one of the biggest rock stars on the planet, the ring, the paparazzi, the legal papers and the hubby himself are all still there, even after you leave Vegas... even if you have absolutely no recollection of the whole thing!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859432._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859433.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Good, respectable, sensible, Portland girl, Evelyn Thomas might have been planning on getting laid, on her 21st birthday, in Vegas... but she certainly hadn't planned on getting married. When she wakes up, hanging like a bitch, on a hotel bathroom floor, with no memory of marrying the gorgeous but mysterious man lying next to her, who is none other than David Ferris, guitarist of rock band, 'Stage Dive', the obvious answer to her problems is an annulment. A no-brainer, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859434._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But what if he <i>does</i> remember the whole thing? And what if he <i>doesn't</i> consider it to be the biggest mistake of his life? <br>And what if Evelyn actually realises she might quite like the sexy, dark, brooding God of rock?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859435.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>David. David. David! *sigh* Awww, he's just to die for. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859436._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He isn't the mean, bad-boy man-whore that most of these rock star romance books deliver us... he's just lovely. He's attentive, sweet, caring, kind and he's hurt. It's clear, from the beginning, that David remembers the events of that fateful night and doesn't regret it like Evelyn does. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859437._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can anybody say 'awwww'?? How can you not want to scoop him up and cuddle him? He wants her to be his wifey and she has no interest in even knowing who he is. Bless his little heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859438._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859439.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Evelyn is brilliant too. She's ordinary and refreshingly rational. It makes a change. She doesn't go flying off of the handle, over-reacting or falling at his feet at the first sign of 'sorry'. She's just a normal girl in a very abnormal situation. And she reacts accordingly. She's strong in her decisions, has self respect but isn't annoyingly stubborn or affected. I really, really liked her and was totally on board with her story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859440._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is told from her POV and the writing is witty, funny and a breath of fresh air. I was giggling by the end of the first page. This is pure easy-reading. <br>I loved that the dialogue felt so real. The responses were things that <i>real</i> people might say. They 'Mmm's and 'yeh's that were used to punctuate a sentence. There was a lot of great banter, too.<br><br>So, post-Vegas, when Evelyn finds herself at David's mansion, in an attempt to escape the hoards of press outside her Portland home, things begin to change.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859441._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved watching Evelyn realise that she actually had feelings for David. And he sure as hell didn't make it a hard job to love him. Honestly, ladies, this guy is <i>so</i> damn cute. He'll do a total warm and fuzzy number on your hearts.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859442._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859443._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don't be fooled though. There are some panty-combusting sex scenes in this book too... just to make sure you don't get a sugar rush from all of the sweet. Ooof, David is haaawt! Evelyn is inexperienced and nervous, and he takes such good care of her, whilst showing her the ropes! Mmmm mmm!<br><br>I have one query... I'd be grateful if somebody could fill me in here... whyyyy is this book called <i>Lick</i>??? It just seemed ever so random, to me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859444._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859445._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is the first in the <i>Stage Dive</i> series. I believe book #2 is Mal's story. Mal is David's oldest friend and the drummer of the band. I absolutely loved his character. He is hilariously funny, kind hearted and a total lad. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859446._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't wait to read more from Kylie Scott. I think we may have found a new favourite fictional rock band, ladies!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429162i/859447._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Lick</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order:</b> <br>Book #1 - Lick<br>Rest of series not released yet.<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Rock star<br>Alcohol induced amnesia<br>Accidental marriage<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> <br>Sexual content. <br><b>Writing:</b> Great<br><br>UK AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Lick-Stage-Dive-1-ebook/dp/B00CY8Q5IM/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1377007546&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=lick+kylie+scott">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Lick-Stage-Di...</a><br>US AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Lick-Stage-Dive-1-ebook/dp/B00CY8Q5IM/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1377007546&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=lick+kylie+scott">http://www.amazon.com/Lick-Stage-Dive...</a><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4913131181432618270"><b>*4.75 "Hi" Stars*</b><br/><br/>Mix together <a href='http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1033643/' rel='nofollow noopener'>What Happens in Vegas</a>, <a href='http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1119646/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Hangover</a> and throw in a smoking hot Rock Star and you have this book. <br/><br/><b>Ev</b> wakes up in Vegas after celebrating her 21st birthday and she can't remember a single thing about the night before. When she sees a strange man, <b>David </b>, in her room she ask him what happened last night.<b> <blockquote> <i>"We got f*cking married." </i>
</blockquote></b><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427869ra/855588.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>SERIES:</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21442559.Lick__Stage_Dive___1_' title='Lick (Stage Dive, #1) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19286623.Lead__Stage_Dive___3_' title='Lead (Stage Dive, #3) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18461986.Untitled__Stage_Dive___4_' title='Untitled (Stage Dive, #4) by Kylie Scott' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png' alt='Untitled (Stage Dive, #4) by Kylie Scott' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Each book will feature a different band member.<br/>Book 1 - David | Book 2 - Mal | Book 3 - Jimmy | Book 4 - ?</span>
  <span id="freeText4913131181432618270" style="display:none"><b>*4.75 "Hi" Stars*</b><br><br>Mix together <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1033643/" rel="nofollow noopener">What Happens in Vegas</a>, <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1119646/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hangover</a> and throw in a smoking hot Rock Star and you have this book. <br><br><b>Ev</b> wakes up in Vegas after celebrating her 21st birthday and she can't remember a single thing about the night before. <div id="review_1107736086" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1107736086" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107736086?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18873617-lick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shy-heroine">shy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=rockstar-hero">rockstar-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107736086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18102550883059600368"><p>
  <strong>4 amnesiac stars</strong>
</p><p>I really enjoyed this opening book of the Stage Dive series from Kylie Scott – it’s charming, funny and deeply romantic full of well-rounded characters and a dynamic plot to keep you engaged right through to the very end.</p><p>Turns out, the old expression ‘What happens in Vegas, stays in Vegas’ probably doesn’t apply if an Elvis impersonator is somehow involved.</p><blockquote>
  <br/>
  <p>
    <em>"Let me get this straight, you don't remember anything?"</em>
    <br/>
    <em>"No," I said, swallowing hard. "What did we </em></p></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText18102550883059600368" style="display:none"><p>
  <strong>4 amnesiac stars</strong>
</p><p>I really enjoyed this opening book of the Stage Dive series from Kylie Scott – it’s charming, funny and deeply romantic full of well-rounded characters and a dynamic plot to keep you engaged right through to the very end.</p><p>Turns out, the old expression ‘What happens in Vegas, stays in Vegas’ probably doesn’t apply if an Elvis impersonator is somehow involved.</p><blockquote>
  <br />
  <p>
    <em>"Let me get this straight, you don't remember anything?"</em>
    <br />
    <em>"No," I said, swallowing hard. "What did we do last night?"</em>
    <br />
    <em>"We got fucking married." he growled.</em>
  </p>
</blockquote><p>Uh oh! Yup, Evelyn has woke up after a night in Vegas remembering very little of the night before and is now throwing up in the hotel bathroom with a very gorgeous, tattooed Adonis checking to see if she is OK.  She has absolutely no recollection of meeting him but it turns out they got married while she was inebriated and, not only that, he’s one quarter of one of the biggest bands on the planet, Stage Dive.</p><p>I so enjoyed this – I don’t think it was taking itself too seriously.  There’s plenty of humour to be found in here along with the angsty romance.  I think it taps into every girl’s fantasy that the Rock God she so adores can ditch his philandering ways and change his bad habits for the one girl who means everything to him – the girl next door type – basically, us the reader.</p><p>David has, of course, had his fair share of disposable groupies over the years and it was sweet to see how he saw something very genuine and refreshingly different in Evelyn.  Turns out that  night she can’t remember meant just about everything to him and, after her initial shock, she allows him to slowly and rather creatively help bring back the memories.</p><p>The book follows the well worn path of boy meets girl, boy and girl fall in love, boys fucks up ,monumentally and loses girl and boy does just about everything in his power to get her back but this isn’t trite at all – it’s well written and the narrative flows beautifully with Kylie Scott’s accomplished style and, with her easy humour, Lick is a charming and engaging read.</p><p>There’s a whole lot of series building going on here with the other members of the band being introduced in all their glory with the promise of some edgy rockstar romances to come as the series progresses. I think it’s a great beginning to a highly promising series and it’s my first read from Kylie Scott.  It won’t be my last.</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="18102550883059600368" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1640300245" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6330408303224044471"><i> 5 'Can I be your wife, David Ferris?' Stars!!! </i><br/><br/><b> “Everything I’d heard about Vegas was true. Bad things happened here, terrible things.” </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468228705ra/19679993.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I have honestly, been going through a rockstar love phase lately, and I love every minute of it! I am three gosh damn years too late on reading this book. I am in such an incredible mood because I was in a terrible book slump for weeks because of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28287721.A_Bloody_Kingdom__Ruthless_People___4_' title='A Bloody Kingdom (Ruthless People, #4) by J.J. McAvoy' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Bloody Kingdom</a> <b> (HIGHLY RECOMMEND!)</b>. I tried so hard to find a book that I didn't start and just put it down beca</span>
  <span id="freeText6330408303224044471" style="display:none"><i> 5 'Can I be your wife, David Ferris?' Stars!!! </i><br><br><b> “Everything I’d heard about Vegas was true. Bad things happened here, terrible things.” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468228705ra/19679993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I have honestly, been going through a rockstar love phase lately, and I love every minute of it! I am three gosh damn years too late on reading this book. I am in such an incredible mood because I was in a terrible book slump for weeks because of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28287721.A_Bloody_Kingdom__Ruthless_People___4_" title="A Bloody Kingdom (Ruthless People, #4) by J.J. McAvoy" rel="nofollow noopener">A Bloody Kingdom</a> <b> (HIGHLY RECOMMEND!)</b>. I tried so hard to find a book that I didn't start and just put it down because It just wasn't as good as the last book I read, but I don't know what made me decide to start reading 'Lick', but I'm so blessed that I did. I hesitated at first because my first thought was 'I hope it isn't a slow start' but boy was I wrong. I loved how the moment you enter this story it gets straight to the point which kept me intrigued! Should I let you know about the story and characters? Yep, right on it... Sorry ;)<br><br>What happens in Vegas stays in Vegas, right? Well, in Evelyn case, what happens in Vegas, leads to you marrying a stud of a rockstar. The story starts off with Evelyn waking up and seeing a stranger beside her <b> (did I mention he was a stud?) </b> and finding out she got married the night before. Uhhh.. did Evelyn panic? Totally. Evelyn couldn't remember anything at all, couldn't remember the long haired sexy blue-eyed stranger in front of her, why he was being so nice, why she had a huge rock on her finger, why her butt was aching (hehe), and why she'd went against all her plans. Evelyn ends up heading back home trying to forget and bury and keep a secret everything that happened in Vegas but little did she know that she would be swarmed with paparazzi ambushing her. Why are paparazzi's ambushing her? Well, that stud that she married was the one and only worldwide known guitarist David Ferris but no big deal, right? <br><br><b> “Wait a minute,” he said, watching me through narrowed eyes. “You’re just messing with me, aren’t you?”<br>“I’m so sorry.”<br>He physically recoiled from me. “Let me get this straight, you don’t remember anything?”<br>“No,” I said, swallowing hard. “What did we do last night?”<br>“We got fucking married,” he growled.” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468230130ra/19680228.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Evelyn didn't know anything about her husband until the paparazzi, and her best friend, Lauren ensure her who he is. Evelyn only knows of Stage Dive (band name) and David because her best friend is beyond obsessed with them but other than that Evelyn is completely blindsided by everything about the band, bandmates, and her husband and the problems/issues that comes with them. <br><br><b> Lauren: I can handle him. Whatever happens, do not break up the band!!!<br>Me: Got it.<br>Lauren: But break his heart. He wrote San Pedro after what’s-her-face cheated on him. That album was BRILLIANT!<br>Me: Promise to leave him a broken quivering mess. <br>Lauren: That’s the spirit. </b><br><br>Just like the album David wrote about his ex, this story was just as <b> BRILLIANT! </b> I loved every second of the story and how It kept me interested to know what happens. But, the primary person that caught my attention the most was Mal. Mal is David's longest friend, and he's part of the band. He was the kindest to Evelyn from the moment he met her, and he wanted nothing more than to help Evelyn &amp; David. Mal made me happy because of how he handled situations and how I he has such a good heart. His personality radiates off the pages. He's just a joy (I love him and can't wait to read his story!). No one knows how many moments Mal made the book a lot better.<br><br><b> “Go on, smile for Uncle Mal. You know you want to.”<br>I smiled half-heartedly.<br>“That’s a bullshit smile, and I’m ashamed of you. You’re not going to fool anyone with that. Try again.”<br>I tried harder, smiling ’til my cheeks hurt.<br>“Damn. Now you just look like you’re in pain.” </b><br><br>I loved the idea that David remembered everything and she didn't so we got to see how he knew her more than she knew him and how he would bring up some things she talked about that night that shocked her because she typically didn't tell people the things she told him. You could say that when things settled down that they just genuinely were at ease and comfortable with each other. The story was an Insta-love, which I'm sort of getting annoyed with in books but in the book I was all up for it. This story will have you understanding both the hero and heroine's side. It will have your heart strings yanking away with how Evelyn and David are with each other. It will have you smiling from cheek to cheek, chuckling at the things that are said from Mal to Evelyn to David. It will have you feeling as if you wished you were part of the book so you could help solve the problems that happen in it. I just love this book because once again it helped me out of my slump and because <b> DAVID FERRIS! </b><br><br><b> Characters: </b><br><i> Everlyn </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468233485ra/19680713.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> He nodded, cocked his head. “So what was your plan? Just kiss me, and see what happened?”<br>“My plan?”<br>“I know about you and your plans. You told me all about how anal you are.”<br>“I told you that?” I was an idiot.<br>“Yeah. You did. You especially told me about the big plan.” He stared down at me, eyes intense.” </b><br><br>Evelyn was an innocent, collected, organized, planned out person. She planned her life away, and anything outside of her plan was uncomfortable for her so you'd expect the thrill and fear for when she met and started to get to know David. What I loved the most about Evelyn was that even though she was innocent, she had a backbone and stood her ground and didn't let anyone push her over. She was witty and adorable, and I just felt protective over her just like David was (it was SO cute how protective he was over her). Another thing that I loved was how David brought the bad in her. He wanted her to get out of her shell. He challenged her and wanted her to be her own person and not to be someone she wasn't to make someone else happy. He just wanted her happy.<br><br><b> A hand smoothed over my hip, and he smiled down at me. “I’ll eat you out whenever you like. You only have to ask.”<br>I smiled back at him. And the smile may have twitched a little at the edges. Talking about this kind of thing was still new to me.<br>“Tell me you liked me licking your gorgeous pussy.”<br>“I said I liked it.”<br>“You’re embarrassed.” David’s brows drew together. There was mischief in his eyes. “You can talk rough sex on hardwood floors but not cunnilingus, hey? Say ‘pussy’.”<br>I rolled my eyes. “Pussy.”<br>“Again. Not as in ‘cat’.” </b><br><br><br><i> David </i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468233485ra/19680714.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> “Why don’t you go back to LA?”<br>Blue eyes watched me warily and he didn’t answer at first. “My wife lives in Portland.” </b><br><br>Davids is the favorite in the group; he writes the songs, plays guitar, bass, drums, sings and he's practically known as the rock n rolls favorite sons. Okay Okay, he was a big deal.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468233485ra/19680715.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But with Evelyn, he was just vulnerable David. Even though David was vulnerable, he was also a jackass at times and the first 50% of the book I liked him a lot, but the last 50% of the book is where my obsession came in. He had the bad boy act all because he was a rock star but David was vulnerable, had huge trust issues and wanted to feel something 'real.' He's been hurt and cheated on many times (dumb whore *rolls eyes*) but marrying Evelyn was the best thing for him. What they had made him believe in love again and what they had was, real. He was a man of a few words but when he did say something, he meant it, and you felt every meaning. Evelyn helped David get out of a dark place and kept him grounded. She allowed him to be happy again, but David comes with a lot of baggage, and sometimes some people can't deal with the lies and heartache. Sometimes the fame isn't what everyone wants. And sometimes you just have to let go and not look back. <br><br><b> I took another step back, and his face hardened to fury. His hands fisted at his sides. “Don’t you dare fucking leave me. You promised!”<br>I didn’t know him at all. I stared at him, transfixed, letting his anger wash over me. It couldn’t hope to pierce the hurt. Not a chance.<br>“You walk out of here, and it’s over. Don’t you fucking think of coming back.”<br>“Okay.” </b><br><br>P.S. Is it weird that I liked how David said "yeah?" After the majority of his sentences? It's weird, isn't it? That's okay. I'll still like it<br><br>P.S. pt.2: Can we get David added onto my 'book husband' list, pronto? *snaps fingers*<br><br><b> Characters together: </b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472163551ra/20160310.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love love love this couple. They gave me everything I would want in a rock star romance. They gave the right amount of emotions, angst, steamy moments, 'I wish I was Evelyn' moments and more. Evelyn &amp; David together are two people who weren't meant to meet, but somehow faith brought them together, it's just in time we'll learn if it was meant to be or just another lesson in both their lives<br><br><b> “Where are we going?” I asked David.<br>“Does it matter? Let’s just drive.” </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468235675ra/19681296.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Do you want a book that will get you out of a book slump?<b> Read this book. </b> Do you want a book that will make you laugh? <b> Read this book. </b> Do you want a book that is the quick read and lighthearted? <b> Read this book. </b> Do you want a rockstar on your boyfriend list? <b> Read this book. </b> Do you want to listen to me? <b> Good, read this book! </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468234606ra/19681058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more reviews! </b><br><div> <a href="https://bookitwithdon.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465508902i/19367462._SX540_.png" alt="Book It With Don" width="275" height="140" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a> </div><br><br>-----------------------------------------<br>(before review)<br><i> "He had long, dark hair falling past his shoulders and sideburns. His eyes were the darkest blue." </i><br><br><b> I already know who my rock star is going to be: <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467977357ra/19652183.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467977357ra/19652185.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>;) </b></span>

  <span id="freeText3081624690504265185" style="display:none">Never in my life, have I woke up from a drunken night next to a super hot guy, who is filthy rich, and has already developed feelings for me..... why has this not happened to me yet.... I keep waiting... and it still isn't happening???😕<br /><br /> Maybe I need to quickly Book me a trip to Vegas....<br /><br />This book just proves my point, if you like fantasy.... you will truly enjoy romance!💕 Even though this book was highly unlikely, to actually happen I still loved it! <br />Eve was a fabulous character... filled with spunk, sass, and clearly some unpredictability.... I truly enjoyed the girl.... David was a good character as well, but I believe I liked her a bit more..<br /> They were very cute together....: and undeniably a perfect match.....<br /><br /> I was happy to see how this book ends.... and I'm absolutely going to read the next book in the series.... I think I might find Mal A little more compelling......<br /><br />Highly recommend this book and all the other books in the series to all fans of love, romance, girls with some sass, and hot musicians😍<br /><br />You can check out all our Flashback Friday reviews along with the audiobook narration at V and my blog...<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://audiokilledthebookmark.com/">https://audiokilledthebookmark.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_661727891" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/661727891" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/661727891?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer661727891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5861185720910189583"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857006._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I need a rock star husband. Pronto. <br/><b>Beware.</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/612591.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yup, with all those steamy moments, it’s as easy as that. <br/><b>David</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857007.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Evelyn</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857008.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>If your looking for romance, steam, humor, and angst in a neatly wrapped and easy to read package, <i>Lick</i> is for you. <br/><br/>Ev has turned twenty-one and her friend, Lauren, has decided it’s time for her to let her hair down and forget about her “plan” for a few days. <br/>That’s how she wakes up in Vegas hungover. <br/>With a husband. <br/>And a huge rock on her finger.<br/>Oh, and don’t forget about the tattoo o</span>
  <span id="freeText5861185720910189583" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857006._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I need a rock star husband. Pronto. <br><b>Beware.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/612591.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yup, with all those steamy moments, it’s as easy as that. <br><b>David</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857007.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Evelyn</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857008.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If your looking for romance, steam, humor, and angst in a neatly wrapped and easy to read package, <i>Lick</i> is for you. <br><br>Ev has turned twenty-one and her friend, Lauren, has decided it’s time for her to let her hair down and forget about her “plan” for a few days. <br>That’s how she wakes up in Vegas hungover. <br>With a husband. <br>And a huge rock on her finger.<br>Oh, and don’t forget about the tattoo on her left butt cheek of his name. Too bad she has no recollection of any of it. <br>Since her husband happens to be David Ferris, a rocks star, what happens in Vegas <i>certainly</i> isn't staying in Vegas.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Let me get this straight, you don’t remember anything?”<br>“No,” I said, swallowing hard. “What did we do last night?”<br>“We got fucking married,” he growled. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I was pleasantly surprised about how much I enjoyed this book. Before reading, I got caught up in all the good reviews and praises that I came in with high expectations, and that never ends well with me. However, <i>Lick</i> was able to hold its own. <br>The beginning was a little slow for me but I quickly got caught up in the story and its characters. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Mal?”<br>“What?”<br>“Close the door down there and lock it,” David yelled. “Don’t you come up here under any circumstances. Not till I tell you it’s okay. Understood?”<br>There was a pause then Mal yelled back. “What if there’s a fire?”<br>“Burn.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>David and Ev were perfect for each other. I loved how they were together. <br><b>David</b> surprised me. For some reason, I pictured him as some asshole rock star but he was really sweet. He had his moments but for the most part I was swooning over him. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “What are we doing? I asked, bewildered.<br>“Spooning. We did it that night for a while. Until you felt sick.”<br>“We spooned?”<br>“Yep,” he said. “Stage two in the memory rehab process, spooning. Now go to sleep.”<br>“I only woke up an hour ago.”<br>He pressed his face into my hair and even threw a leg over mine for good measure, pinning me down. “Bad luck. I’m tired and I wanna spoon. With you. And the way I figure it, you owe me. So we’re spooining.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b>Ev</b> was awesome. I loved her personality and <b>especially</b> how she would think before she would act. <br>One thing I really respected was how she didn’t search the web for information on the band and David. I mean, I don’t know how many stories I read that the heroine would investigate the hero and it always led to disaster. <br>She trusted that David would tell her everything when he was ready. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “Love isn’t always smooth or straightforward. It can be messy and painful,” he said. “Doesn’t mean it isn’t still the most incredible thing that can ever happen to you.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Another thing I liked about this book was how Kylie Scott described the famous/ rock star lifestyle. She didn’t make it out to be rainbows and unicorns but it wasn’t too graphic and off-putting. <br><br><i>Lick</i> had me laughing, smiling, and fanning myself but it didn’t make me <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> everything. When <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ev found David “cheating”, it was sad but it didn’t <b>devastate</b> me <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. It was the only major thing that lacked for me. I wanted to really <b>feel</b> everything like I was there and not just reading what was happening. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428331i/857009._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nonetheless, I truly enjoyed this book and can’t wait for the second one. <br>*Fingers crossed for book 2 being Mal’s*<br><br>A solid 4 entertaining stars.<br>★★★★</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="5861185720910189583" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=famous">famous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25192009-rag?shelf=did-i-get-married">did-i-get-married</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1272583376" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7651710306116041104"><b>4 <i>'Lick Me'</i> Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsozrua0fa.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431150852i/14796262._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpsozrua0fa.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Imagine waking up in the morning with a hangover, really bad headache, feeling sick, sleeping on the bathroom, no memory, and on top of that <i>married!</i> <br/>What would you do if you woke up, remembering nothing but taking shots at midnight and seeing a big ass ring on your finger? <br/><br/>Yup my friend, that's exactly what happened to Evelyn Thomas. All she ever wanted was to celebrate her twenty-first birthday in Las Vegas. But what she ended up with was a bad hung over, a tattoo on her </span>
  <span id="freeText7651710306116041104" style="display:none"><b>4 <i>'Lick Me'</i> Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsozrua0fa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431150852i/14796262._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsozrua0fa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Imagine waking up in the morning with a hangover, really bad headache, feeling sick, sleeping on the bathroom, no memory, and on top of that <i>married!</i> <br>What would you do if you woke up, remembering nothing but taking shots at midnight and seeing a big ass ring on your finger? <br><br>Yup my friend, that's exactly what happened to Evelyn Thomas. All she ever wanted was to celebrate her twenty-first birthday in Las Vegas. But what she ended up with was a bad hung over, a tattoo on her ass check, and a ring that probable costs more than she can ever imagine.She doesn't remember anything. And when she sees her "husband", hell she doesn't even know his name. She then finds out that she married a rock star. David-Fucking-Ferris.<br><br><b>"congratulations. You’re married to a rock star.”</b><br><br>Lets just say when she found out she didn't take the news very well.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431150853ra/14796263.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like I said about Channing Tatum<br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpssuoctrwn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431150853i/14796264.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpssuoctrwn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Same goes to Davie, if I woke up married to him I won't question it. Who would?<br><br>David remembers everything. He is mad though because Ev doesn't remember a damn thing about that night. It make Ev even more frustrated that she can't remember.<br><br><b>“It’s not fair that you remember and I don’t.”<br>“No,” he said, his voice hard, cold, in a way I hadn’t heard it. He loomed over me, jaw set.<br>“It’s not fair that I remember and you don’t, Evelyn.”</b><br><br>She doesn't want this marriage. She has a career (that she doesn't even like) ahead of her. She wants a divorce. She never not knows where she'll go or what will she do.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpscl9oxdpt.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431150853i/14796265._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpscl9oxdpt.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Paparazzi and the fans led them to going somewhere while all this shit cools down. They went to David's house to get away. That's when they realized they needed a second chance, to see where things might go.<br> <br><b>Truth was, I wanted him. All of him. The good and the bad and the bits in between. I wanted him more than I’d ever wanted anything before in my life.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392852153ra/8622752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ev realized that she is falling. That he's not as bad as she thought he was. She might even fall for him. <br><br><b>I didn’t know David then. But I was beginning to now. And the more we talked, the more I liked him.</b><br><br>And their sex is off the chain. Especially the showers they be having.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431150853ra/14796266.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Speaking of showers, I think I need a cold one.<br><br>David was just so hot, sweet, and tender. I loved him. Loved the way he loves Ev and everything about him.<br><br><b>“I married you, Evelyn, because you made sense to me. We make sense. We’re a whole lot better together than apart. You notice that?”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385950320ra/7264170.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So what will happen when Davies past comes crashing down?<br><br>Read to find out. If you haven't read it, then I RECOMMEND!<br><br>The only thing that caused 4 stars not 5 is that Ev never remembered. I wanted her to remember the night she got married but she didn't so that's the only problem I have.<br>Overall...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1430403004ra/14709807.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_656079817" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656079817" />
    <a title="Jen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5962787-jen"><img alt="Jen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563496869p2/5962787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/656079817?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18047274-lick">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=first-book-read-from-author">first-book-read-from-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=good-girl-meets-bad-boy">good-girl-meets-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer656079817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13498130183725377032"><i>
  <b>All I could do was stare. Given my current condition, he was just too much. The hair, face. Body, ink, all of it. Someone needed to invent a word superlative enough to describe him.</b>
</i><br/><br/>When Evelyn wakes up on the floor of a Vegas hotel bathroom with the hangover from hell, the last thing she expects to hear from the hot but unfamiliar looking inked up hottie taking care of her is that they’re married. Say what? The poor girl can’t remember anything after tequila shots and this sexy stranger’s cl</span>
  <span id="freeText13498130183725377032" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>All I could do was stare. Given my current condition, he was just too much. The hair, face. Body, ink, all of it. Someone needed to invent a word superlative enough to describe him.</b>
</i><br /><br />When Evelyn wakes up on the floor of a Vegas hotel bathroom with the hangover from hell, the last thing she expects to hear from the hot but unfamiliar looking inked up hottie taking care of her is that they’re married. Say what? The poor girl can’t remember anything after tequila shots and this sexy stranger’s claiming to be her husband? Even without the monster hangover, that’s a messed up situation to find yourself in. When David, hot guitar player extraordinaire, figures out Evelyn has absolutely no recollection of the amazing night they shared he storms out promising to take care of the situation. That plan works for about twelve hours until the press gets wind of the nuptials.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>This part of LA was clearly a colony for ill-mannered douches.</b>
</i><br /><br />Retreating to David’s temporary home in LA does not go well for the couple. Jealous bitches abound, smarmy lawyers and their ass hat ways and some band mates that seem less than enthused about the new girl in their lives lead Ev and David to head to his house in Monterey in order to try and make sense of the situation. And so begins new couple phase for Evelyn and David.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>”You don’t want me to lie and say everything’s always fucking unicorns and rainbows, do you?” “Maybe. Yes. People are going to know these are about me. I have a reputation as a constant delight to protect.”</b>
</i><br /><br />This entire book was a delight. I’ve read <i>a lot</i> of rock star books and this one was one of the most entertaining to read. Most have way too much repetitive sex and not enough story for me, which is where this one differs. Is there plenty of hot sex to be had? You bet, but the story doesn’t suffer for it. The book’s told from Evelyn’s POV and she’s awesome! She’s curvy, “unyielding” and “big boned” to quote her, but she never puts herself down and, once she finds out how much her man loves her body, enjoys using those curves to her advantage<br /><br /><i>
  <b>”With great breasts comes great responsibility.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Her inner monologues are hilarious and I could absolutely understand why David fell fast and hard for her. In his world of suck ups and people who always want something from him, she has to be considered a breath of fresh air. David’s no slouch, either. He’s possessive, sweet, funny but definitely flawed. His luck with the women in his life standing by him is crap and this takes its toll on the relationship more than once. These two go through some serious relationship stuff in the course of about a month and they both have some serious come to Jesus moments before the eventual HEA. That being said, if you can’t handle the insta-love thing this book may not be for you. <br /><br />I finished this book an hour ago and I’m still smiling. I can’t think of a better compliment for a book than that. I’m hoping Ms. Scott’s a quick writer because I’m ready for the next book in this series NOW!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13498130183725377032" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w6RrPg2WT6ivBVnKY21/bZnIGS+3rfFpKRvGaf241X8KolL/x4o94BwECmXYka3g3vJYF19AQVTb/QOTqU17yQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8IzRkWwWBHl+2DuVtFvl+7ND6Al3fI7M3Ks21hu5WpY5iuhQpgp2Mc3ZaDoPpzd29HmpMZ+RPvEuTfMsT0z0IA==')})
  }
